<a name="ps_1771769515081"></a>
## Prompt Set (ps_1771769515081)

**Time:** 2026-02-22T14:11:55.081Z
**Duration:** 0ms
**Tool Calls:** 24

### Task - 2026-02-22 14:11:55 UTC [15:11:55 CEST]

**User Request:** # Documentation Style Guide

Enforce consistent styling for documentation artifacts (PlantUML, Mermaid, markdown, PNG diagrams).

## Instructions

When creating or modifying documentation artifacts, follow these guidelines strictly.

---

## PlantUML Diagrams (.puml)

### File Naming Convention

**CRITICAL**: Use kebab-case, descriptive names. NEVER use incremental suffixes.

**Correct**:
- `health-verification-flow.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components.puml`

**WRONG** (constraint violation):
- `health-verification-flow-2.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture-v2.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components-new.puml`

If updating an existing diagram, **modify the existing file** rather than creating a new version.

### Standard Style Include

All PlantUML files MUST include the standard style at the top:

```plantuml
@startuml diagram-name
!include _standard-style.puml

' ... diagram content ...

@enduml
```

The style file is located at:
- `docs/puml/_standard-style.puml`
- `docs/presentation/puml/_standard-style.puml`

### Layout Guidelines

1. **Prefer vertical layouts** - Avoid excessive width that requires horizontal scrolling
2. **Use `top to bottom direction`** for most diagrams
3. **Use `left to right direction`** only for sequence diagrams or when horizontal flow is semantically meaningful
4. **Group related components** using packages or rectangles

### Component Stereotypes

Use these stereotypes for consistent coloring:

| Stereotype | Color | Use For |
|------------|-------|---------|
| `<<api>>` | Light Blue | API endpoints, REST interfaces |
| `<<core>>` | Light Green | Core business logic |
| `<<storage>>` | Light Yellow | Databases, file storage |
| `<<cli>>` | Light Pink | Command-line interfaces |
| `<<util>>` | Light Gray | Utility/helper components |
| `<<agent>>` | Soft Blue | AI agents, autonomous components |
| `<<infra>>` | Light <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> | Infrastructure components |
| `<<external>>` | Neutral Gray | External systems |

### Arrow Macros

Use defined macros for consistent arrow styling:

```plantuml
SYNC_LINE     ' Red solid line - synchronous calls
ASYNC_LINE    ' Green dashed - async/event-based
DATA_LINE     ' <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> solid - data flow
CONTROL_LINE  ' Purple solid - control flow
OPTIONAL_LINE ' Gray dotted - optional paths
```

---

## PNG Generation

### Generating PNGs from PlantUML

Use the PlantUML JAR or online service:

```bash
# Local generation (preferred)
java -jar plantuml.jar -tpng docs/puml/diagram-name.puml

# Or use the docs script if available
./scripts/generate-diagrams.sh
```

### PNG Naming

PNG files should match their source PUML file:
- `health-verification-flow.puml` â†’ `health-verification-flow.png`

### Output Location

PNGs should be generated to:
- `docs/images/` - For markdown documentation references
- `docs/presentation/png/` - For presentation diagrams

---

## Mermaid Diagrams

### Inline in Markdown

Use fenced code blocks with `mermaid` language:

```markdown
```mermaid
graph TD
    A[Start] --> B{Decision}
    B -->|Yes| C[Action]
    B -->|No| D[End]
```
```

### Style Guidelines

1. Use clear, descriptive node labels
2. Keep diagrams focused - split large diagrams into multiple
3. Use subgraphs for logical grouping
4. Prefer `graph TD` (top-down) over `graph LR` (left-right) for readability

---

## Markdown Documentation

### File Naming

- Use kebab-case: `api-quota-checker.md`
- Use `README.md` for directory index files
- Never use spaces or special characters

### Structure

1. Start with H1 title matching the topic
2. Include brief overview paragraph
3. Use H2 for major sections
4. Use H3 for subsections
5. Include code examples where applicable

### Links

- Use relative paths for internal links: `[Status Line](./status-line.md)`
- Use absolute URLs for external links
- Verify links work before committing

---

## Validation Workflow

Before committing documentation changes:

1. **PlantUML**: Verify syntax by generating PNG
2. **Mermaid**: Preview in VS Code or GitHub
3. **Markdown**: Check rendering in preview
4. **Links**: Verify all internal links work
5. **Images**: Ensure referenced images exist

---

## Common Violations to Avoid

1. **Incremental naming** (`-2`, `-v2`, `-new` suffixes)
2. **Missing style include** in PlantUML
3. **Horizontal-heavy layouts** causing scroll
4. **Orphaned images** (PNG without source PUML)
5. **Broken internal links**
6. **Inconsistent component colors** (not using stereotypes)

---

## Quick Reference

| Artifact | Location | Naming | Style |
|----------|----------|--------|-------|
| PlantUML | `docs/puml/` | kebab-case.puml | Include `_standard-style.puml` |
| PNG | `docs/images/` | match-source.png | Generated from PUML |
| Markdown | `docs/*/` | kebab-case.md | H1 title, H2 sections |
| Mermaid | Inline | N/A | graph TD preferred |

**Tool:** Task
**Input:** ```json
{
  "description": "Find docs about billing/status",
  "subagent_type": "Explore",
  "prompt": "Find all documentation files (*.md) in the /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding project that mention any of: api-quota-checker, status line billing, provider credits, spending tracking, tmux status, BudgetTracker, billing scraper, admin API key, management key, prepaid credits, xAI management. Search in docs/, README.md, and any other .md files. Be thorough - check docs/, docs/architecture/, docs/guides/, docs/reference/, and root-level markdown files. Return the full list of matching file paths with the relevant context of what each file covers.",
  "model": "haiku"
}
```

PNGs should be generated to:
- `docs/images/` - For markdown documentation references
- `docs/presentation/png/` - For presentation diagrams

---

## Mermaid Diagrams

### Inline in Markdown

Use fenced code blocks with `mermaid` language:

```markdown
```mermaid
graph TD
    A[Start] --> B{Decision}
    B -->|Yes| C[Action]
    B -->|No| D[End]
```
```

### Style Guidelines

1. Use clear, descriptive node labels
2. Keep diagrams focused - split large diagrams into multiple
3. Use subgraphs for logical grouping
4. Prefer `graph TD` (top-down) over `graph LR` (left-right) for readability

---

## Markdown Documentation

### File Naming

- Use kebab-case: `api-quota-checker.md`
- Use `README.md` for directory index files
- Never use spaces or special characters

### Structure

1. Start with H1 title matching the topic
2. Include brief overview paragraph
3. Use H2 for major sections
4. Use H3 for subsections
5. Include code examples where applicable

### Links

- Use relative paths for internal links: `[Status Line](./status-line.md)`
- Use absolute URLs for external links
- Verify links work before committing

---

## Validation Workflow

Before committing documentation changes:

1. **PlantUML**: Verify syntax by generating PNG
2. **Mermaid**: Preview in VS Code or GitHub
3. **Markdown**: Check rendering in preview
4. **Links**: Verify all internal links work
5. **Images**: Ensure referenced images exist

---

## Common Violations to Avoid

1. **Incremental naming** (`-2`, `-v2`, `-new` suffixes)
2. **Missing style include** in PlantUML
3. **Horizontal-heavy layouts** causing scroll
4. **Orphaned images** (PNG without source PUML)
5. **Broken internal links**
6. **Inconsistent component colors** (not using stereotypes)

---

| Artifact | Location | Naming | Style |

| PNG | `docs/images/` | match-source.png | Generated from PUML |
| Markdown | `docs/*/` | kebab-case.md | H1 title, H2 sections |
| Mermaid | Inline | N/A | graph TD preferred |

**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>h-system/status-line.md"
}

### Read - 2026-02-22 14:11:55 UTC [15:11:55 CEST]

**User Request:** # Documentation Style Guide

Enforce consistent styling for documentation artifacts (PlantUML, Mermaid, markdown, PNG diagrams).

## Instructions

When creating or modifying documentation artifacts, follow these guidelines strictly.

---

## PlantUML Diagrams (.puml)

### File Naming Convention

**CRITICAL**: Use kebab-case, descriptive names. NEVER use incremental suffixes.

**Correct**:
- `health-verification-flow.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components.puml`

**WRONG** (constraint violation):
- `health-verification-flow-2.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture-v2.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components-new.puml`

If updating an existing diagram, **modify the existing file** rather than creating a new version.

### Standard Style Include

All PlantUML files MUST include the standard style at the top:

```plantuml
@startuml diagram-name
!include _standard-style.puml

' ... diagram content ...

@enduml
```

The style file is located at:
- `docs/puml/_standard-style.puml`
- `docs/presentation/puml/_standard-style.puml`

### Layout Guidelines

1. **Prefer vertical layouts** - Avoid excessive width that requires horizontal scrolling
2. **Use `top to bottom direction`** for most diagrams
3. **Use `left to right direction`** only for sequence diagrams or when horizontal flow is semantically meaningful
4. **Group related components** using packages or rectangles

### Component Stereotypes

Use these stereotypes for consistent coloring:

| Stereotype | Color | Use For |
|------------|-------|---------|
| `<<api>>` | Light Blue | API endpoints, REST interfaces |
| `<<core>>` | Light Green | Core business logic |
| `<<storage>>` | Light Yellow | Databases, file storage |
| `<<cli>>` | Light Pink | Command-line interfaces |
| `<<util>>` | Light Gray | Utility/helper components |
| `<<agent>>` | Soft Blue | AI agents, autonomous components |
| `<<infra>>` | Light <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> | Infrastructure components |
| `<<external>>` | Neutral Gray | External systems |

### Arrow Macros

Use defined macros for consistent arrow styling:

```plantuml
SYNC_LINE     ' Red solid line - synchronous calls
ASYNC_LINE    ' Green dashed - async/event-based
DATA_LINE     ' <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> solid - data flow
CONTROL_LINE  ' Purple solid - control flow
OPTIONAL_LINE ' Gray dotted - optional paths
```

---

## PNG Generation

### Generating PNGs from PlantUML

Use the PlantUML JAR or online service:

```bash
# Local generation (preferred)
java -jar plantuml.jar -tpng docs/puml/diagram-name.puml

# Or use the docs script if available
./scripts/generate-diagrams.sh
```

### PNG Naming

PNG files should match their source PUML file:
- `health-verification-flow.puml` â†’ `health-verification-flow.png`

### Output Location

PNGs should be generated to:
- `docs/images/` - For markdown documentation references
- `docs/presentation/png/` - For presentation diagrams

---

## Mermaid Diagrams

### Inline in Markdown

Use fenced code blocks with `mermaid` language:

```markdown
```mermaid
graph TD
    A[Start] --> B{Decision}
    B -->|Yes| C[Action]
    B -->|No| D[End]
```
```

### Style Guidelines

1. Use clear, descriptive node labels
2. Keep diagrams focused - split large diagrams into multiple
3. Use subgraphs for logical grouping
4. Prefer `graph TD` (top-down) over `graph LR` (left-right) for readability

---

### File Naming

- Use kebab-case: `api-quota-checker.md`

### Edit - 2026-02-22 14:11:55 UTC [15:11:55 CEST]

**User Request:** # Documentation Style Guide

Enforce consistent styling for documentation artifacts (PlantUML, Mermaid, markdown, PNG diagrams).

## Instructions

When creating or modifying documentation artifacts, follow these guidelines strictly.

---

## PlantUML Diagrams (.puml)

### File Naming Convention

**CRITICAL**: Use kebab-case, descriptive names. NEVER use incremental suffixes.

**Correct**:
- `health-verification-flow.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components.puml`

**WRONG** (constraint violation):
- `health-verification-flow-2.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture-v2.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components-new.puml`

If updating an existing diagram, **modify the existing file** rather than creating a new version.

### Standard Style Include

All PlantUML files MUST include the standard style at the top:

```plantuml
@startuml diagram-name
!include _standard-style.puml

' ... diagram content ...

@enduml
```

The style file is located at:
- `docs/puml/_standard-style.puml`
- `docs/presentation/puml/_standard-style.puml`

### Layout Guidelines

1. **Prefer vertical layouts** - Avoid excessive width that requires horizontal scrolling
2. **Use `top to bottom direction`** for most diagrams
3. **Use `left to right direction`** only for sequence diagrams or when horizontal flow is semantically meaningful
4. **Group related components** using packages or rectangles

### Component Stereotypes

Use these stereotypes for consistent coloring:

| Stereotype | Color | Use For |
|------------|-------|---------|
| `<<api>>` | Light Blue | API endpoints, REST interfaces |
| `<<core>>` | Light Green | Core business logic |
| `<<storage>>` | Light Yellow | Databases, file storage |
| `<<cli>>` | Light Pink | Command-line interfaces |
| `<<util>>` | Light Gray | Utility/helper components |
| `<<agent>>` | Soft Blue | AI agents, autonomous components |
| `<<infra>>` | Light <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> | Infrastructure components |
| `<<external>>` | Neutral Gray | External systems |

### Arrow Macros

Use defined macros for consistent arrow styling:

```plantuml
SYNC_LINE     ' Red solid line - synchronous calls
ASYNC_LINE    ' Green dashed - async/event-based
DATA_LINE     ' <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> solid - data flow
CONTROL_LINE  ' Purple solid - control flow
OPTIONAL_LINE ' Gray dotted - optional paths
```

---

## PNG Generation

### Generating PNGs from PlantUML

Use the PlantUML JAR or online service:

```bash
# Local generation (preferred)
java -jar plantuml.jar -tpng docs/puml/diagram-name.puml

# Or use the docs script if available
./scripts/generate-diagrams.sh
```

### PNG Naming

PNG files should match their source PUML file:
- `health-verification-flow.puml` â†’ `health-verification-flow.png`

### Output Location

PNGs should be generated to:
- `docs/images/` - For markdown documentation references
- `docs/presentation/png/` - For presentation diagrams

---

## Mermaid Diagrams

### Inline in Markdown

Use fenced code blocks with `mermaid` language:

```markdown
```mermaid
graph TD
    A[Start] --> B{Decision}
    B -->|Yes| C[Action]
    B -->|No| D[End]
```
```

### Style Guidelines

1. Use clear, descriptive node labels
2. Keep diagrams focused - split large diagrams into multiple
3. Use subgraphs for logical grouping
4. Prefer `graph TD` (top-down) over `graph LR` (left-right) for readability

---

## Markdown Documentation

### File Naming

- Use kebab-case: `api-quota-checker.md`
- Use `README.md` for directory index files
- Never use spaces or special characters

### Structure

1. Start with H1 title matching the topic
2. Include brief overview paragraph
3. Use H2 for major sections
4. Use H3 for subsections
5. Include code examples where applicable

### Links

- Use relative paths for internal links: `[Status Line](./status-line.md)`
- Use absolute URLs for external links
- Verify links work before committing

---

## Validation Workflow

Before committing documentation changes:

1. **PlantUML**: Verify syntax by generating PNG
2. **Mermaid**: Preview in VS Code or GitHub
3. **Markdown**: Check rendering in preview
4. **Links**: Verify all internal links work
5. **Images**: Ensure referenced images exist

---

## Common Violations to Avoid

1. **Incremental naming** (`-2`, `-v2`, `-new` suffixes)
2. **Missing style include** in PlantUML
3. **Horizontal-heavy layouts** causing scroll
4. **Orphaned images** (PNG without source PUML)
5. **Broken internal links**
6. **Inconsistent component colors** (not using stereotypes)

---

## Quick Reference

| Artifact | Location | Naming | Style |
|----------|----------|--------|-------|
| PlantUML | `docs/puml/` | kebab-case.puml | Include `_standard-style.puml` |
| PNG | `docs/images/` | match-source.png | Generated from PUML |
| Markdown | `docs/*/` | kebab-case.md | H1 title, H2 sections |
| Mermaid | Inline | N/A | graph TD preferred |

**Tool:** Edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>h-system/status-line.md",
  "old_string": "### API Quota Monitoring\n\nThe status line displays LLM provider availability using a simple, consistent format.\n\n**Format**: `[Provider$X ...]` or `[Providerâ— ...]`\n\n**Provider Abbreviations**:\n- `Gq` - X.AI Grok (free credits: $25)\n\n**Display Logic**:\n\n| Scenario | Display | Meaning |\n|----------|---------|---------|\n| Monthly billing (Groq) | `Gq$2JAN` | $2 spent in January |\n| Prepaid credits configured | `A$18` | $18 remaining of prepaid amount |\n| Free tier (Groq, <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED>) | `Gqâ—` | Available (rate-limited only) |\n| No admin key | `Oâ—‹` | Cannot get usage data |\n\n**Pie Chart Symbols** (for availability):\n- `â—` (full) -   "new_string": "### API Quota Monitoring\n\nThe status line displays **live spending data** for all LLM providers using automatic API-based tracking.\n\n**Format**: `[Provider$X ...]`\n\n**Provider Abbreviations and Data Sources**:\n\n| Abbrev | Provider | Data Source | Env Vars Required |\n|--------|----------|-------------|-------------------|\n| `Gq` | Groq | BudgetTracker self-tracking (`.data/llm-usage-costs.json`) | `GROQ_API_KEY` |\n| `Ggl` | <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> Gemini | Free tier (no tracking needed) | `GEMINI_API_KEY` |\n| `A` | Anthropic | Admin API (`/v1/organizations/cost_report`) | `ANTHROPIC_ADMIN_API_KEY` |\n| `O` | OpenAI | Admin API (`/v1/organization/costs`) | `OPENAI_ADMIN_API_KEY` |\n| `X` | X.AI Grok | Management API (`prepaid/balance`) | `XAI_MANAGEMENT_KEY` + `XAI_TEAM_ID` |\n\n**Display Logic**:\n\n| Scenario | Display | Meaning |\n|----------|---------|---------|\n| Admin API: spend data | `A$2` | $2 spent this month (live from API) |\n| Admin API: with prepaid credits | `A$18` | $18 remaining of prepaid amount |\n| Monthly billing (Groq) | `Gq$0FEB` | $0 spent in February (auto-tracked) |\n| Management API (xAI) | `X$25` | $25 remaining prepaid balance |\n| Free tier (<COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED>) | `Gglâ—` | Available (rate-limited only) |\n| No admin key configured | `Oâ—‹` | Cannot get usage data |\n\n**Pie Chart Symbols** (used when percentage-based display applies):\n- `â—` (full) - Groq requires no setup (automatic self-tracking).\n\n**Configuration**:\n\nProvider credits in `config/live-logging-config.json` are used as fallbacks or for prepaid balance display:\n\n```json\n\"provider_credits\": {\n  \"groq\": {\n    \"billingType\": \"monthly\",\n    \"monthlySpend\": 0,\n    \"billingMonth\": \"FEB\",\n    \"spendLimit\": null\n  },\n  \"anthropic\": { \"prepaidCredits\": 0 },\n  \"openai\": { \"prepaidCredits\": null },\n  \"xai\": { \"prepaidCredits\": 25 }\n}\n```\n\n**Groq Self-Tracking**:\n\nGroq has no billing API. Instead, the Docker-based `BudgetTracker` (`src/inference/BudgetTracker.js`) tracks per-provider costs from every LLM call and writes them to `.data/llm-usage-costs.json`. The `api-quota-checker.js` reads this file for the Groq spend amount. The Playwright billing scraper is automatically bypassed when self-tracking data exists.\n\n**API Keys / Management Keys** (in `.env`):\n\n| Variable | Provider | Where to Get It |\n|----------|----------|----------------|\n| `ANTHROPIC_ADMIN_API_KEY` | Anthropic | console.anthropic.com â†’ Settings â†’ Admin API Keys |\n| `OPENAI_ADMIN_API_KEY` | OpenAI | platform.openai.com/settings/organization/admin-keys |\n| `XAI_MANAGEMENT_KEY` | xAI | console.x.ai â†’ Settings â†’ Management Keys |\n| `XAI_TEAM_ID` | xAI | console.x.ai team settings URL |\n| _(none needed)_ | Groq | Automatic via BudgetTracker self-tracking |\n\n**Environment Loading**: The `status-line-fast.cjs` cache reader automatically loads `.env` from the repo root, so admin keys defined there are available to all status line processes without needing to export them in the shell."

| Stereotype | Color | Use For |
|------------|-------|---------|
| `<<api>>` | Light Blue | API endpoints, REST interfaces |
| `<<core>>` | Light Green | Core business logic |
| `<<storage>>` | Light Yellow | Databases, file storage |
| `<<cli>>` | Light Pink | Command-line interfaces |
| `<<util>>` | Light Gray | Utility/helper components |
| `<<agent>>` | Soft Blue | AI agents, autonomous components |
| `<<infra>>` | Light <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> | Infrastructure components |
| `<<external>>` | Neutral Gray | External systems |

### Arrow Macros

Use defined macros for consistent arrow styling:

```plantuml
SYNC_LINE     ' Red solid line - synchronous calls
ASYNC_LINE    ' Green dashed - async/event-based
DATA_LINE     ' <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> solid - data flow
CONTROL_LINE  ' Purple solid - control flow
OPTIONAL_LINE ' Gray dotted - optional paths
```

---

## PNG Generation

### Generating PNGs from PlantUML

Use the PlantUML JAR or online service:

```bash
# Local generation (preferred)
java -jar plantuml.jar -tpng docs/puml/diagram-name.puml

# Or use the docs script if available
./scripts/generate-diagrams.sh
```

### PNG Naming

PNG files should match their source PUML file:
- `health-verification-flow.puml` â†’ `health-verification-flow.png`

### Output Location

PNGs should be generated to:
- `docs/images/` - For markdown documentation references
- `docs/presentation/png/` - For presentation diagrams

---

## Mermaid Diagrams

### Inline in Markdown

Use fenced code blocks with `mermaid` language:

```markdown
```mermaid
graph TD
    A[Start] --> B{Decision}
    B -->|Yes| C[Action]
    B -->|No| D[End]
```
```

### Style Guidelines

1. Use clear, descriptive node labels
2. Keep diagrams focused - split large diagrams into multiple
3. Use subgraphs for logical grouping
4. Prefer `graph TD` (top-down) over `graph LR` (left-right) for readability

---

## Markdown Documentation

### File Naming

- Use kebab-case: `api-quota-checker.md`
- Use `README.md` for directory index files
- Never use spaces or special characters

### Structure

1. Start with H1 title matching the topic
2. Include brief overview paragraph
3. Use H2 for major sections
4. Use H3 for subsections
5. Include code examples where applicable

### Links

- Use relative paths for internal links: `[Status Line](./status-line.md)`
- Use absolute URLs for external links
- Verify links work before committing

---

## Validation Workflow

Before committing documentation changes:

1. **PlantUML**: Verify syntax by generating PNG
2. **Mermaid**: Preview in VS Code or GitHub
3. **Markdown**: Check rendering in preview
4. **Links**: Verify all internal links work
5. **Images**: Ensure referenced images exist

---

## Common Violations to Avoid

1. **Incremental naming** (`-2`, `-v2`, `-new` suffixes)
2. **Missing style include** in PlantUML
3. **Horizontal-heavy layouts** causing scroll
4. **Orphaned images** (PNG without source PUML)
5. **Broken internal links**
6. **Inconsistent component colors** (not using stereotypes)

---

## Quick Reference

| Artifact | Location | Naming | Style |
|----------|----------|--------|-------|
| PlantUML | `docs/puml/` | kebab-case.puml | Include `_standard-style.puml` |
| PNG | `docs/images/` | match-source.png | Generated from PUML |
| Markdown | `docs/*/` | kebab-case.md | H1 title, H2 sections |
| Mermaid | Inline | N/A | graph TD preferred |

**Tool:** Edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "replace_all": true,
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>h-system/status-line.md",
  "old_string": "[Gq$2JAN A$18]",
  "new_string": "[Gq$0FEB A$0 O$0 X$25]"
}
```

**Result:** âœ… Success
**Output:** ```
The file <AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>h-system/status-line.md has been updated. All occurrences of '[Gq$2JAN A$18]' were successfully replaced with '[Gq$0FEB A$0 O$0 X$25]'.
```

**User Request:** # Documentation Style Guide

Enforce consistent styling for documentation artifacts (PlantUML, Mermaid, markdown, PNG diagrams).

## Instructions

When creating or modifying documentation artifacts, follow these guidelines strictly.

---

## PlantUML Diagrams (.puml)

### File Naming Convention

**CRITICAL**: Use kebab-case, descriptive names. NEVER use incremental suffixes.

**Correct**:
- `health-verification-flow.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components.puml`

**WRONG** (constraint violation):
- `health-verification-flow-2.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture-v2.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components-new.puml`

If updating an existing diagram, **modify the existing file** rather than creating a new version.

### Standard Style Include

All PlantUML files MUST include the standard style at the top:

```plantuml
@startuml diagram-name
!include _standard-style.puml

' ... diagram content ...

@enduml
```

The style file is located at:
- `docs/puml/_standard-style.puml`
- `docs/presentation/puml/_standard-style.puml`

### Layout Guidelines

1. **Prefer vertical layouts** - Avoid excessive width that requires horizontal scrolling
2. **Use `top to bottom direction`** for most diagrams
3. **Use `left to right direction`** only for sequence diagrams or when horizontal flow is semantically meaningful
4. **Group related components** using packages or rectangles

### Component Stereotypes

Use these stereotypes for consistent coloring:

| Stereotype | Color | Use For |
|------------|-------|---------|
| `<<api>>` | Light Blue | API endpoints, REST interfaces |
| `<<core>>` | Light Green | Core business logic |
| `<<storage>>` | Light Yellow | Databases, file storage |
| `<<cli>>` | Light Pink | Command-line interfaces |
| `<<util>>` | Light Gray | Utility/helper components |
| `<<agent>>` | Soft Blue | AI agents, autonomous components |
| `<<infra>>` | Light <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> | Infrastructure components |
| `<<external>>` | Neutral Gray | External systems |

### Arrow Macros

Use defined macros for consistent arrow styling:

```plantuml
SYNC_LINE     ' Red solid line - synchronous calls
ASYNC_LINE    ' Green dashed - async/event-based
DATA_LINE     ' <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> solid - data flow
CONTROL_LINE  ' Purple solid - control flow
OPTIONAL_LINE ' Gray dotted - optional paths
```

- `health-verification-flow.puml` â†’ `health-verification-flow.png`

- Never use spaces or special characters

### Structure

1. Start with H1 title matching the topic
2. Include brief overview paragraph
3. Use H2 for major sections
4. Use H3 for subsections
5. Include code examples where applicable

### Links

- Use relative paths for internal links: `[Status Line](./status-line.md)`
- Use absolute URLs for external links
- Verify links work before committing

---

## Validation Workflow

Before committing documentation changes:

1. **PlantUML**: Verify syntax by generating PNG
2. **Mermaid**: Preview in VS Code or GitHub
3. **Markdown**: Check rendering in preview
4. **Links**: Verify all internal links work
5. **Images**: Ensure referenced images exist

---

## Common Violations to Avoid

1. **Incremental naming** (`-2`, `-v2`, `-new` suffixes)
2. **Missing style include** in PlantUML
3. **Horizontal-heavy layouts** causing scroll
4. **Orphaned images** (PNG without source PUML)
5. **Broken internal links**
6. **Inconsistent component colors** (not using stereotypes)

---

## Quick Reference

| Artifact | Location | Naming | Style |
|----------|----------|--------|-------|
| PlantUML | `docs/puml/` | kebab-case.puml | Include `_standard-style.puml` |
| PNG | `docs/images/` | match-source.png | Generated from PUML |
| Markdown | `docs/*/` | kebab-case.md | H1 title, H2 sections |
| Mermaid | Inline | N/A | graph TD preferred |

`billingMonth` - 3-letter month abbreviation (JAN, FEB, etc.)\n  - `spendLimit` - Optional spend limit for warnings\n\n**Admin API Keys** (required for real-time usage tracking):\n\n- **Anthropic**: `ANTHROPIC_ADMIN_API_KEY` - Get at console.anthropic.com â†’ Settings â†’ Admin API Keys\n- **OpenAI**: `OPENAI_ADMIN_API_KEY` - Get at platform.openai.com/settings/organization/admin-keys\n- **Groq**: No public billing API yet - update `monthlySpend` manually from console.groq.com",

No manual spend updates needed after initial key setup.\n\n### Format\n\n`[Provider$X ...]` â€” dollar amounts show live spend or remaining balance.\n\n### Provider Data Sources\n\n| Abbrev | Provider | Data Source | Setup |\n|--------|----------|-------------|-------|\n| `Gq` | Groq | BudgetTracker self-tracking | Automatic (no key needed) |\n| `Ggl` | <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> Gemini | Free tier (no tracking) | `GEMINI_API_KEY` |\n| `A` | Anthropic | Admin API (cost report) | `ANTHROPIC_ADMIN_API_KEY` |\n| `O` | OpenAI | Admin API (costs) | `OPENAI_ADMIN_API_KEY` |\n| `X` | X.AI Grok | Management API (balance) | `XAI_MANAGEMENT_KEY` + `XAI_TEAM_ID` |\n\n### Display Logic\n\n| Scenario | Display | Meaning |\n|----------|---------|---------|\n| Admin API: spend data | `A$2` | $2 spent this month (live) |\n| Admin API: with prepaid credits | `A$18` | $18 remaining of prepaid |\n| Monthly self-tracked (Groq) | `Gq$0FEB` | $0 spent in February |\n| Management API (xAI) | `X$25` | $25 remaining balance |\n| Free tier (<COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED>) | `Gglâ—` | Available (rate-limited) |\n| No admin key configured | `Oâ—‹` | Cannot get usage data |\n\n### Pie Chart Symbols\n\nUsed when percentage-based display applies (prepaid credits configured):\n\n| Symbol | Name | Remaining |\n|--------|------|-----------|\n| `â—` | Full | >87.5% |\n| `â—•` | Three-quarters | 62.5-87.5% |\n| `â—` | Half | 37.5-62.5% |\n| `â—”` | <USER_ID_REDACTED> | 12.5-37.5% |\n| `â—‹` | Empty | <12.5% or no data |\n\n### Setup\n\nRun the interactive setup script to configure API keys (one-time):\n\n```bash\nnode scripts/setup-api-keys.js\n```\n\nEach key is validated with a test API call before saving to `.env`. Groq requires no setup.\n\n### API Keys Reference\n\n| Variable | Provider | Where to Get It |\n|----------|----------|----------------|\n| `ANTHROPIC_ADMIN_API_KEY` | Anthropic | console.anthropic.com â†’ Settings â†’ Admin API Keys |\n| `OPENAI_ADMIN_API_KEY` | OpenAI | platform.openai.com/settings/organization/admin-keys |\n| `XAI_MANAGEMENT_KEY` | xAI | console.x.ai â†’ Settings â†’ Management Keys |\n| `XAI_TEAM_ID` | xAI | console.x.ai team settings URL |\n\n### How Groq Self-Tracking Works\n\nGroq has no billing API. The Docker-based `BudgetTracker` (`src/inference/BudgetTracker.js`) tracks costs from every LLM call and periodically writes to `.data/llm-usage-costs.json` (debounced, atomic write). The `api-quota-checker.js` reads this file for Groq spend. The legacy Playwright billing scraper is automatically bypassed when self-tracking data exists.\n\n### Configuration\n\nProvider credits in `config/live-logging-config.json` serve as fallbacks:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"provider_credits\": {\n    \"groq\": {\n      \"billingType\": \"monthly\",\n      \"monthlySpend\": 0,\n      \"billingMonth\": \"FEB\",\n      \"spendLimit\": null\n    },\n    \"anthropic\": { \"prepaidCredits\": 0 },\n    \"openai\": { \"prepaidCredits\": null },\n    \"xai\": { \"prepaidCredits\": 25 }\n  }\n}\n```"

### Edit - 2026-02-22 14:11:55 UTC [15:11:55 CEST]

**User Request:** # Documentation Style Guide

Enforce consistent styling for documentation artifacts (PlantUML, Mermaid, markdown, PNG diagrams).

## Instructions

When creating or modifying documentation artifacts, follow these guidelines strictly.

---

## PlantUML Diagrams (.puml)

### File Naming Convention

**CRITICAL**: Use kebab-case, descriptive names. NEVER use incremental suffixes.

**Correct**:
- `health-verification-flow.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components.puml`

**WRONG** (constraint violation):
- `health-verification-flow-2.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture-v2.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components-new.puml`

If updating an existing diagram, **modify the existing file** rather than creating a new version.

### Standard Style Include

All PlantUML files MUST include the standard style at the top:

```plantuml
@startuml diagram-name
!include _standard-style.puml

' ... diagram content ...

@enduml
```

The style file is located at:
- `docs/puml/_standard-style.puml`
- `docs/presentation/puml/_standard-style.puml`

### Layout Guidelines

1. **Prefer vertical layouts** - Avoid excessive width that requires horizontal scrolling
2. **Use `top to bottom direction`** for most diagrams
3. **Use `left to right direction`** only for sequence diagrams or when horizontal flow is semantically meaningful
4. **Group related components** using packages or rectangles

### Component Stereotypes

Use these stereotypes for consistent coloring:

| Stereotype | Color | Use For |
|------------|-------|---------|
| `<<api>>` | Light Blue | API endpoints, REST interfaces |
| `<<core>>` | Light Green | Core business logic |
| `<<storage>>` | Light Yellow | Databases, file storage |
| `<<cli>>` | Light Pink | Command-line interfaces |
| `<<util>>` | Light Gray | Utility/helper components |
| `<<agent>>` | Soft Blue | AI agents, autonomous components |
| `<<infra>>` | Light <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> | Infrastructure components |
| `<<external>>` | Neutral Gray | External systems |

### Arrow Macros

Use defined macros for consistent arrow styling:

```plantuml
SYNC_LINE     ' Red solid line - synchronous calls
ASYNC_LINE    ' Green dashed - async/event-based
DATA_LINE     ' <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> solid - data flow
CONTROL_LINE  ' Purple solid - control flow
OPTIONAL_LINE ' Gray dotted - optional paths
```

---

## PNG Generation

### Generating PNGs from PlantUML

Use the PlantUML JAR or online service:

```bash
# Local generation (preferred)
java -jar plantuml.jar -tpng docs/puml/diagram-name.puml

# Or use the docs script if available
./scripts/generate-diagrams.sh
```

### PNG Naming

PNG files should match their source PUML file:
- `health-verification-flow.puml` â†’ `health-verification-flow.png`

### Output Location

PNGs should be generated to:
- `docs/images/` - For markdown documentation references
- `docs/presentation/png/` - For presentation diagrams

---

## Mermaid Diagrams

### Inline in Markdown

Use fenced code blocks with `mermaid` language:

```markdown
```mermaid
graph TD
    A[Start] --> B{Decision}
    B -->|Yes| C[Action]
    B -->|No| D[End]
```
```

### Style Guidelines

1. Use clear, descriptive node labels
2. Keep diagrams focused - split large diagrams into multiple
3. Use subgraphs for logical grouping
4. Prefer `graph TD` (top-down) over `graph LR` (left-right) for readability

---

## Markdown Documentation

### File Naming

- Use kebab-case: `api-quota-checker.md`
- Use `README.md` for directory index files
- Never use spaces or special characters

### Structure

1. Start with H1 title matching the topic
2. Include brief overview paragraph
3. Use H2 for major sections
4. Use H3 for subsections
5. Include code examples where applicable

### Links

- Use relative paths for internal links: `[Status Line](./status-line.md)`
- Use absolute URLs for external links
- Verify links work before committing

---

Before committing documentation changes:

1. **PlantUML**: Verify syntax by generating PNG

3. **Markdown**: Check rendering in preview
4. **Links**: Verify all internal links work
5. **Images**: Ensure referenced images exist

---

2. **Missing style include** in PlantUML
3. **Horizontal-heavy layouts** causing scroll
4. **Orphaned images** (PNG without source PUML)
5. **Broken internal links**
6. **Inconsistent component colors** (not using stereotypes)

**CRITICAL**: Use kebab-case, descriptive names. NEVER use incremental suffixes.

**Correct**:
- `health-verification-flow.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components.puml`

**WRONG** (constraint violation):
- `health-verification-flow-2.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture-v2.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components-new.puml`

If updating an existing diagram, **modify the existing file** rather than creating a new version.

### Standard Style Include

All PlantUML files MUST include the standard style at the top:

```plantuml
@startuml diagram-name
!include _standard-style.puml

' ... diagram content ...

@enduml
```

The style file is located at:
- `docs/puml/_standard-style.puml`
- `docs/presentation/puml/_standard-style.puml`

### Layout Guidelines

1. **Prefer vertical layouts** - Avoid excessive width that requires horizontal scrolling
2. **Use `top to bottom direction`** for most diagrams
3. **Use `left to right direction`** only for sequence diagrams or when horizontal flow is semantically meaningful
4. **Group related components** using packages or rectangles

### Component Stereotypes

Use these stereotypes for consistent coloring:

| Stereotype | Color | Use For |
|------------|-------|---------|
| `<<api>>` | Light Blue | API endpoints, REST interfaces |
| `<<core>>` | Light Green | Core business logic |
| `<<storage>>` | Light Yellow | Databases, file storage |
| `<<cli>>` | Light Pink | Command-line interfaces |
| `<<util>>` | Light Gray | Utility/helper components |
| `<<agent>>` | Soft Blue | AI agents, autonomous components |
| `<<infra>>` | Light <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> | Infrastructure components |
| `<<external>>` | Neutral Gray | External systems |

### Arrow Macros

Use defined macros for consistent arrow styling:

```plantuml
SYNC_LINE     ' Red solid line - synchronous calls
ASYNC_LINE    ' Green dashed - async/event-based
DATA_LINE     ' <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> solid - data flow
CONTROL_LINE  ' Purple solid - control flow
OPTIONAL_LINE ' Gray dotted - optional paths
```

---

## PNG Generation

### Generating PNGs from PlantUML

Use the PlantUML JAR or online service:

```bash
# Local generation (preferred)
java -jar plantuml.jar -tpng docs/puml/diagram-name.puml

# Or use the docs script if available
./scripts/generate-diagrams.sh
```

### PNG Naming

PNG files should match their source PUML file:
- `health-verification-flow.puml` â†’ `health-verification-flow.png`

### Output Location

PNGs should be generated to:
- `docs/images/` - For markdown documentation references
- `docs/presentation/png/` - For presentation diagrams

---

## Mermaid Diagrams

### Inline in Markdown

Use fenced code blocks with `mermaid` language:

```markdown
```mermaid
graph TD
    A[Start] --> B{Decision}
    B -->|Yes| C[Action]
    B -->|No| D[End]
```
```

### Style Guidelines

1. Use clear, descriptive node labels
2. Keep diagrams focused - split large diagrams into multiple
3. Use subgraphs for logical grouping
4. Prefer `graph TD` (top-down) over `graph LR` (left-right) for readability

---

## Markdown Documentation

### File Naming

- Use kebab-case: `api-quota-checker.md`
- Use `README.md` for directory index files
- Never use spaces or special characters

### Structure

1. Start with H1 title matching the topic
2. Include brief overview paragraph
3. Use H2 for major sections
4. Use H3 for subsections
5. Include code examples where applicable

### Links

- Use relative paths for internal links: `[Status Line](./status-line.md)`
- Use absolute URLs for external links
- Verify links work before committing

---

## Validation Workflow

Before committing documentation changes:

1. **PlantUML**: Verify syntax by generating PNG
2. **Mermaid**: Preview in VS Code or GitHub
3. **Markdown**: Check rendering in preview
4. **Links**: Verify all internal links work
5. **Images**: Ensure referenced images exist

---

## Common Violations to Avoid

1. **Incremental naming** (`-2`, `-v2`, `-new` suffixes)
2. **Missing style include** in PlantUML
3. **Horizontal-heavy layouts** causing scroll
4. **Orphaned images** (PNG without source PUML)
5. **Broken internal links**
6. **Inconsistent component colors** (not using stereotypes)

---

## Quick Reference

| Artifact | Location | Naming | Style |
|----------|----------|--------|-------|
| PlantUML | `docs/puml/` | kebab-case.puml | Include `_standard-style.puml` |
| PNG | `docs/images/` | match-source.png | Generated from PUML |
| Markdown | `docs/*/` | kebab-case.md | H1 title, H2 sections |
| Mermaid | Inline | N/A | graph TD preferred |

**Tool:** Edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>h-system/README.md",
  "old_string": "- `[Gq$0FEB A$0 O$0 X$25]` - API quota status (Groq $2 spent in Jan, etc.)",
  "new_string": "- `[Gq$0FEB A$0 O$0 X$25]` - API quota (live spend/balance from APIs)"
}
```

**Result:** âœ… Success
**Output:** ```
The file <AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>h-system/README.md has been updated successfully.
```

- Use kebab-case: `api-quota-checker.md`
- Use `README.md` for directory index files
- Never use spaces or special characters

### Structure

1. Start with H1 title matching the topic
2. Include brief overview paragraph
3. Use H2 for major sections
4. Use H3 for subsections
5. Include code examples where applicable

### Links

- Use relative paths for internal links: `[Status Line](./status-line.md)`
- Use absolute URLs for external links
- Verify links work before committing

---

## Validation Workflow

Before committing documentation changes:

1. **PlantUML**: Verify syntax by generating PNG
2. **Mermaid**: Preview in VS Code or GitHub
3. **Markdown**: Check rendering in preview
4. **Links**: Verify all internal links work
5. **Images**: Ensure referenced images exist

---

## Common Violations to Avoid

1. **Incremental naming** (`-2`, `-v2`, `-new` suffixes)
2. **Missing style include** in PlantUML
3. **Horizontal-heavy layouts** causing scroll
4. **Orphaned images** (PNG without source PUML)
5. **Broken internal links**
6. **Inconsistent component colors** (not using stereotypes)

---

## Quick Reference

| Artifact | Location | Naming | Style |
|----------|----------|--------|-------|
| PlantUML | `docs/puml/` | kebab-case.puml | Include `_standard-style.puml` |
| PNG | `docs/images/` | match-source.png | Generated from PUML |
| Markdown | `docs/*/` | kebab-case.md | H1 title, H2 sections |
| Mermaid | Inline | N/A | graph TD preferred |

### Read - 2026-02-22 14:11:55 UTC [15:11:55 CEST]

**User Request:** # Documentation Style Guide

Enforce consistent styling for documentation artifacts (PlantUML, Mermaid, markdown, PNG diagrams).

## Instructions

When creating or modifying documentation artifacts, follow these guidelines strictly.

---

## PlantUML Diagrams (.puml)

### File Naming Convention

**CRITICAL**: Use kebab-case, descriptive names. NEVER use incremental suffixes.

**Correct**:
- `health-verification-flow.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components.puml`

**WRONG** (constraint violation):
- `health-verification-flow-2.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture-v2.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components-new.puml`

If updating an existing diagram, **modify the existing file** rather than creating a new version.

### Standard Style Include

All PlantUML files MUST include the standard style at the top:

```plantuml
@startuml diagram-name
!include _standard-style.puml

' ... diagram content ...

@enduml
```

The style file is located at:
- `docs/puml/_standard-style.puml`
- `docs/presentation/puml/_standard-style.puml`

### Layout Guidelines

1. **Prefer vertical layouts** - Avoid excessive width that requires horizontal scrolling
2. **Use `top to bottom direction`** for most diagrams
3. **Use `left to right direction`** only for sequence diagrams or when horizontal flow is semantically meaningful
4. **Group related components** using packages or rectangles

### Component Stereotypes

Use these stereotypes for consistent coloring:

| Stereotype | Color | Use For |
|------------|-------|---------|
| `<<api>>` | Light Blue | API endpoints, REST interfaces |
| `<<core>>` | Light Green | Core business logic |
| `<<storage>>` | Light Yellow | Databases, file storage |
| `<<cli>>` | Light Pink | Command-line interfaces |
| `<<util>>` | Light Gray | Utility/helper components |
| `<<agent>>` | Soft Blue | AI agents, autonomous components |
| `<<infra>>` | Light <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> | Infrastructure components |
| `<<external>>` | Neutral Gray | External systems |

### Arrow Macros

Use defined macros for consistent arrow styling:

```plantuml
SYNC_LINE     ' Red solid line - synchronous calls
ASYNC_LINE    ' Green dashed - async/event-based
DATA_LINE     ' <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> solid - data flow
CONTROL_LINE  ' Purple solid - control flow
OPTIONAL_LINE ' Gray dotted - optional paths
```

---

## PNG Generation

### Generating PNGs from PlantUML

Use the PlantUML JAR or online service:

```bash
# Local generation (preferred)
java -jar plantuml.jar -tpng docs/puml/diagram-name.puml

# Or use the docs script if available
./scripts/generate-diagrams.sh
```

### PNG Naming

PNG files should match their source PUML file:
- `health-verification-flow.puml` â†’ `health-verification-flow.png`

### Output Location

PNGs should be generated to:
- `docs/images/` - For markdown documentation references
- `docs/presentation/png/` - For presentation diagrams

---

## Mermaid Diagrams

### Inline in Markdown

Use fenced code blocks with `mermaid` language:

```markdown
```mermaid
graph TD
    A[Start] --> B{Decision}
    B -->|Yes| C[Action]
    B -->|No| D[End]
```
```

### Style Guidelines

1. Use clear, descriptive node labels
2. Keep diagrams focused - split large diagrams into multiple
3. Use subgraphs for logical grouping
4. Prefer `graph TD` (top-down) over `graph LR` (left-right) for readability

---

6. **Inconsistent component colors** (not using stereotypes)

| Mermaid | Inline | N/A | graph TD preferred |

### Read - 2026-02-22 14:11:55 UTC [15:11:55 CEST]

**User Request:** # Documentation Style Guide

Enforce consistent styling for documentation artifacts (PlantUML, Mermaid, markdown, PNG diagrams).

## Instructions

When creating or modifying documentation artifacts, follow these guidelines strictly.

---

## PlantUML Diagrams (.puml)

### File Naming Convention

**CRITICAL**: Use kebab-case, descriptive names. NEVER use incremental suffixes.

**Correct**:
- `health-verification-flow.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components.puml`

**WRONG** (constraint violation):
- `health-verification-flow-2.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture-v2.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components-new.puml`

If updating an existing diagram, **modify the existing file** rather than creating a new version.

### Standard Style Include

All PlantUML files MUST include the standard style at the top:

```plantuml
@startuml diagram-name
!include _standard-style.puml

' ... diagram content ...

@enduml
```

The style file is located at:
- `docs/puml/_standard-style.puml`
- `docs/presentation/puml/_standard-style.puml`

### Layout Guidelines

1. **Prefer vertical layouts** - Avoid excessive width that requires horizontal scrolling
2. **Use `top to bottom direction`** for most diagrams
3. **Use `left to right direction`** only for sequence diagrams or when horizontal flow is semantically meaningful
4. **Group related components** using packages or rectangles

### Component Stereotypes

Use these stereotypes for consistent coloring:

| Stereotype | Color | Use For |
|------------|-------|---------|
| `<<api>>` | Light Blue | API endpoints, REST interfaces |
| `<<core>>` | Light Green | Core business logic |
| `<<storage>>` | Light Yellow | Databases, file storage |
| `<<cli>>` | Light Pink | Command-line interfaces |
| `<<util>>` | Light Gray | Utility/helper components |
| `<<agent>>` | Soft Blue | AI agents, autonomous components |
| `<<infra>>` | Light <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> | Infrastructure components |
| `<<external>>` | Neutral Gray | External systems |

### Arrow Macros

Use defined macros for consistent arrow styling:

```plantuml
SYNC_LINE     ' Red solid line - synchronous calls
ASYNC_LINE    ' Green dashed - async/event-based
DATA_LINE     ' <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> solid - data flow
CONTROL_LINE  ' Purple solid - control flow
OPTIONAL_LINE ' Gray dotted - optional paths
```

---

## PNG Generation

### Generating PNGs from PlantUML

Use the PlantUML JAR or online service:

```bash
# Local generation (preferred)
java -jar plantuml.jar -tpng docs/puml/diagram-name.puml

# Or use the docs script if available
./scripts/generate-diagrams.sh
```

### PNG Naming

PNG files should match their source PUML file:
- `health-verification-flow.puml` â†’ `health-verification-flow.png`

### Output Location

PNGs should be generated to:
- `docs/images/` - For markdown documentation references
- `docs/presentation/png/` - For presentation diagrams

---

## Mermaid Diagrams

### Inline in Markdown

Use fenced code blocks with `mermaid` language:

```markdown
```mermaid
graph TD
    A[Start] --> B{Decision}
    B -->|Yes| C[Action]
    B -->|No| D[End]
```
```

### Style Guidelines

1. Use clear, descriptive node labels
2. Keep diagrams focused - split large diagrams into multiple
3. Use subgraphs for logical grouping
4. Prefer `graph TD` (top-down) over `graph LR` (left-right) for readability

---

## Markdown Documentation

### File Naming

- Use kebab-case: `api-quota-checker.md`
- Use `README.md` for directory index files
- Never use spaces or special characters

### Structure

1. Start with H1 title matching the topic
2. Include brief overview paragraph
3. Use H2 for major sections
4. Use H3 for subsections
5. Include code examples where applicable

### Links

- Use relative paths for internal links: `[Status Line](./status-line.md)`
- Use absolute URLs for external links
- Verify links work before committing

---

## Validation Workflow

Before committing documentation changes:

1. **PlantUML**: Verify syntax by generating PNG
2. **Mermaid**: Preview in VS Code or GitHub
3. **Markdown**: Check rendering in preview
4. **Links**: Verify all internal links work
5. **Images**: Ensure referenced images exist

---

## Common Violations to Avoid

1. **Incremental naming** (`-2`, `-v2`, `-new` suffixes)
2. **Missing style include** in PlantUML
3. **Horizontal-heavy layouts** causing scroll
4. **Orphaned images** (PNG without source PUML)
5. **Broken internal links**
6. **Inconsistent component colors** (not using stereotypes)

---

## Quick Reference

| Artifact | Location | Naming | Style |
|----------|----------|--------|-------|
| PlantUML | `docs/puml/` | kebab-case.puml | Include `_standard-style.puml` |
| PNG | `docs/images/` | match-source.png | Generated from PUML |
| Markdown | `docs/*/` | kebab-case.md | H1 title, H2 sections |
| Mermaid | Inline | N/A | graph TD preferred |

**Tool:** Read
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/docs-content/guides/status-line.md"
}
```

**Result:** âœ… Success
**Output:** ```
     1â†’# Status Line Complete Guide
     2â†’
     3â†’Real-time visual indicators of system health and development activity rendered via the unified tmux status bar. ```plantuml

!include _standard-style.puml

' ... diagram content ...

@enduml
```

The style file is located at:
- `docs/puml/_standard-style.puml`
- `docs/presentation/puml/_standard-style.puml`

### Layout Guidelines

1. **Prefer vertical layouts** - Avoid excessive width that requires horizontal scrolling
2. **Use `top to bottom direction`** for most diagrams
3. **Use `left to right direction`** only for sequence diagrams or when horizontal flow is semantically meaningful
4. **Group related components** using packages or rectangles

### Component Stereotypes

Use these stereotypes for consistent coloring:

| Stereotype | Color | Use For |
|------------|-------|---------|
| `<<api>>` | Light Blue | API endpoints, REST interfaces |
| `<<core>>` | Light Green | Core business logic |
| `<<storage>>` | Light Yellow | Databases, file storage |
| `<<cli>>` | Light Pink | Command-line interfaces |
| `<<util>>` | Light Gray | Utility/helper components |
| `<<agent>>` | Soft Blue | AI agents, autonomous components |
| `<<infra>>` | Light <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> | Infrastructure components |
| `<<external>>` | Neutral Gray | External systems |

### Arrow Macros

Use defined macros for consistent arrow styling:

```plantuml
SYNC_LINE     ' Red solid line - synchronous calls
ASYNC_LINE    ' Green dashed - async/event-based
DATA_LINE     ' <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> solid - data flow
CONTROL_LINE  ' Purple solid - control flow
OPTIONAL_LINE ' Gray dotted - optional paths
```

---

## PNG Generation

### Generating PNGs from PlantUML

Use the PlantUML JAR or online service:

```bash
# Local generation (preferred)
java -jar plantuml.jar -tpng docs/puml/diagram-name.puml

# Or use the docs script if available
./scripts/generate-diagrams.sh
```

### PNG Naming

PNG files should match their source PUML file:
- `health-verification-flow.puml` â†’ `health-verification-flow.png`

### Output Location

PNGs should be generated to:
- `docs/images/` - For markdown documentation references
- `docs/presentation/png/` - For presentation diagrams

---

## Mermaid Diagrams

### Inline in Markdown

Use fenced code blocks with `mermaid` language:

```markdown
```mermaid
graph TD
    A[Start] --> B{Decision}
    B -->|Yes| C[Action]
    B -->|No| D[End]
```
```

### Style Guidelines

1. Use clear, descriptive node labels
2. Keep diagrams focused - split large diagrams into multiple
3. Use subgraphs for logical grouping
4. Prefer `graph TD` (top-down) over `graph LR` (left-right) for readability

---

## Markdown Documentation

### File Naming

- Use kebab-case: `api-quota-checker.md`
- Use `README.md` for directory index files
- Never use spaces or special characters

### Structure

1. Start with H1 title matching the topic
2. Include brief overview paragraph
3. Use H2 for major sections
4. Use H3 for subsections
5. Include code examples where applicable

### Links

- Use relative paths for internal links: `[Status Line](./status-line.md)`
- Use absolute URLs for external links
- Verify links work before committing

---

## Validation Workflow

Before committing documentation changes:

1. **PlantUML**: Verify syntax by generating PNG
2. **Mermaid**: Preview in VS Code or GitHub
3. **Markdown**: Check rendering in preview
4. **Links**: Verify all internal links work
5. **Images**: Ensure referenced images exist

---

## Common Violations to Avoid

1. **Incremental naming** (`-2`, `-v2`, `-new` suffixes)
2. **Missing style include** in PlantUML
3. **Horizontal-heavy layouts** causing scroll
4. **Orphaned images** (PNG without source PUML)
5. **Broken internal links**
6. **Inconsistent component colors** (not using stereotypes)

---

## Quick Reference

| Artifact | Location | Naming | Style |
|----------|----------|--------|-------|
| PlantUML | `docs/puml/` | kebab-case.puml | Include `_standard-style.puml` |
| PNG | `docs/images/` | match-source.png | Generated from PUML |
| Markdown | `docs/*/` | kebab-case.md | H1 title, H2 sections |
| Mermaid | Inline | N/A | graph TD preferred |

Instead, the Docker-based `BudgetTracker` (`src/inference/BudgetTracker.js`) tracks per-provider costs from every LLM call and writes them to `.data/llm-usage-costs.json`. The `api-quota-checker.js` reads this file for the Groq spend amount. The Playwright billing scraper is automatically bypassed when self-tracking data exists.\n\n**API Keys / Management Keys** (in `.env`):\n\n| Variable | Provider | Where to Get It |\n|----------|----------|----------------|\n| `ANTHROPIC_ADMIN_API_KEY` | Anthropic | console.anthropic.com â†’ Settings â†’ Admin API Keys |\n| `OPENAI_ADMIN_API_KEY` | OpenAI | platform.openai.com/settings/organization/admin-keys |\n| `XAI_MANAGEMENT_KEY` | xAI | console.x.ai â†’ Settings â†’ Management Keys |\n| `XAI_TEAM_ID` | xAI | console.x.ai team settings URL |\n| _(none needed)_ | Groq | Automatic via BudgetTracker self-tracking |\n\n**Environment Loading**: The `status-line-fast.cjs` cache reader automatically loads `.env` from the repo root, so admin keys defined there are available to all status line processes without needing to export them in the shell."

### Edit - 2026-02-22 14:11:55 UTC [15:11:55 CEST]

**User Request:** # Documentation Style Guide

Enforce consistent styling for documentation artifacts (PlantUML, Mermaid, markdown, PNG diagrams).

## Instructions

When creating or modifying documentation artifacts, follow these guidelines strictly.

---

## PlantUML Diagrams (.puml)

### File Naming Convention

**CRITICAL**: Use kebab-case, descriptive names. NEVER use incremental suffixes.

**Correct**:
- `health-verification-flow.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components.puml`

**WRONG** (constraint violation):
- `health-verification-flow-2.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture-v2.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components-new.puml`

If updating an existing diagram, **modify the existing file** rather than creating a new version.

### Standard Style Include

All PlantUML files MUST include the standard style at the top:

```plantuml
@startuml diagram-name
!include _standard-style.puml

' ... diagram content ...

@enduml
```

The style file is located at:
- `docs/puml/_standard-style.puml`
- `docs/presentation/puml/_standard-style.puml`

### Layout Guidelines

1. **Prefer vertical layouts** - Avoid excessive width that requires horizontal scrolling
2. **Use `top to bottom direction`** for most diagrams
3. **Use `left to right direction`** only for sequence diagrams or when horizontal flow is semantically meaningful
4. **Group related components** using packages or rectangles

### Component Stereotypes

Use these stereotypes for consistent coloring:

| Stereotype | Color | Use For |
|------------|-------|---------|
| `<<api>>` | Light Blue | API endpoints, REST interfaces |
| `<<core>>` | Light Green | Core business logic |
| `<<storage>>` | Light Yellow | Databases, file storage |
| `<<cli>>` | Light Pink | Command-line interfaces |
| `<<util>>` | Light Gray | Utility/helper components |
| `<<agent>>` | Soft Blue | AI agents, autonomous components |
| `<<infra>>` | Light <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> | Infrastructure components |
| `<<external>>` | Neutral Gray | External systems |

### Arrow Macros

Use defined macros for consistent arrow styling:

```plantuml
SYNC_LINE     ' Red solid line - synchronous calls
ASYNC_LINE    ' Green dashed - async/event-based
DATA_LINE     ' <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> solid - data flow
CONTROL_LINE  ' Purple solid - control flow
OPTIONAL_LINE ' Gray dotted - optional paths
```

---

## PNG Generation

### Generating PNGs from PlantUML

Use the PlantUML JAR or online service:

```bash
# Local generation (preferred)
java -jar plantuml.jar -tpng docs/puml/diagram-name.puml

# Or use the docs script if available
./scripts/generate-diagrams.sh
```

### PNG Naming

PNG files should match their source PUML file:
- `health-verification-flow.puml` â†’ `health-verification-flow.png`

### Output Location

PNGs should be generated to:
- `docs/images/` - For markdown documentation references
- `docs/presentation/png/` - For presentation diagrams

---

## Mermaid Diagrams

### Inline in Markdown

Use fenced code blocks with `mermaid` language:

```markdown
```mermaid
graph TD
    A[Start] --> B{Decision}
    B -->|Yes| C[Action]
    B -->|No| D[End]
```
```

### Style Guidelines

1. Use clear, descriptive node labels
2. Keep diagrams focused - split large diagrams into multiple
3. Use subgraphs for logical grouping
4. Prefer `graph TD` (top-down) over `graph LR` (left-right) for readability

---

## Markdown Documentation

### File Naming

- Use kebab-case: `api-quota-checker.md`
- Use `README.md` for directory index files
- Never use spaces or special characters

### Structure

1. Start with H1 title matching the topic
2. Include brief overview paragraph
3. Use H2 for major sections
4. Use H3 for subsections
5. Include code examples where applicable

### Links

- Use absolute URLs for external links

Before committing documentation changes:

1. **PlantUML**: Verify syntax by generating PNG
2. **Mermaid**: Preview in VS Code or GitHub

5. **Images**: Ensure referenced images exist

## Common Violations to Avoid

2. **Missing style include** in PlantUML
3. **Horizontal-heavy layouts** causing scroll
4. **Orphaned images** (PNG without source PUML)
5. **Broken internal links**
6. **Inconsistent component colors** (not using stereotypes)

2. Keep diagrams focused - split large diagrams into multiple
3. Use subgraphs for logical grouping
4. Prefer `graph TD` (top-down) over `graph LR` (left-right) for readability

---

## Markdown Documentation

### File Naming

- Use kebab-case: `api-quota-checker.md`
- Use `README.md` for directory index files
- Never use spaces or special characters

### Structure

1. Start with H1 title matching the topic
2. Include brief overview paragraph
3. Use H2 for major sections
4. Use H3 for subsections
5. Include code examples where applicable

### Links

- Use relative paths for internal links: `[Status Line](./status-line.md)`
- Use absolute URLs for external links
- Verify links work before committing

---

## Validation Workflow

Before committing documentation changes:

1. **PlantUML**: Verify syntax by generating PNG
2. **Mermaid**: Preview in VS Code or GitHub
3. **Markdown**: Check rendering in preview
4. **Links**: Verify all internal links work
5. **Images**: Ensure referenced images exist

---

## Common Violations to Avoid

1. **Incremental naming** (`-2`, `-v2`, `-new` suffixes)
2. **Missing style include** in PlantUML
3. **Horizontal-heavy layouts** causing scroll
4. **Orphaned images** (PNG without source PUML)
5. **Broken internal links**
6. **Inconsistent component colors** (not using stereotypes)

---

## Quick Reference

| Artifact | Location | Naming | Style |
|----------|----------|--------|-------|
| PlantUML | `docs/puml/` | kebab-case.puml | Include `_standard-style.puml` |
| PNG | `docs/images/` | match-source.png | Generated from PUML |
| Markdown | `docs/*/` | kebab-case.md | H1 title, H2 sections |
| Mermaid | Inline | N/A | graph TD preferred |

**Tool:** Edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "replace_all": true,
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>h-system/status-line.md",
  "old_string": "[Gq$2JAN A$18]",
  "new_string": "[Gq$0FEB A$0 O$0 X$25]"
}
```

**Result:** âœ… Success
**Output:** ```
The file <AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>h-system/status-line.md has been updated. All occurrences of '[Gq$2JAN A$18]' were successfully replaced with '[Gq$0FEB A$0 O$0 X$25]'.
```

### Edit - 2026-02-22 14:11:55 UTC [15:11:55 CEST]

**User Request:** # Documentation Style Guide

Enforce consistent styling for documentation artifacts (PlantUML, Mermaid, markdown, PNG diagrams).

## Instructions

When creating or modifying documentation artifacts, follow these guidelines strictly.

---

## PlantUML Diagrams (.puml)

### File Naming Convention

**CRITICAL**: Use kebab-case, descriptive names. NEVER use incremental suffixes.

**Correct**:
- `health-verification-flow.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components.puml`

**WRONG** (constraint violation):
- `health-verification-flow-2.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture-v2.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components-new.puml`

If updating an existing diagram, **modify the existing file** rather than creating a new version.

### Standard Style Include

All PlantUML files MUST include the standard style at the top:

```plantuml
@startuml diagram-name
!include _standard-style.puml

' ... diagram content ...

@enduml
```

The style file is located at:
- `docs/puml/_standard-style.puml`
- `docs/presentation/puml/_standard-style.puml`

### Layout Guidelines

1. **Prefer vertical layouts** - Avoid excessive width that requires horizontal scrolling
2. **Use `top to bottom direction`** for most diagrams
3. **Use `left to right direction`** only for sequence diagrams or when horizontal flow is semantically meaningful
4. **Group related components** using packages or rectangles

### Component Stereotypes

Use these stereotypes for consistent coloring:

| Stereotype | Color | Use For |
|------------|-------|---------|
| `<<api>>` | Light Blue | API endpoints, REST interfaces |
| `<<core>>` | Light Green | Core business logic |
| `<<storage>>` | Light Yellow | Databases, file storage |
| `<<cli>>` | Light Pink | Command-line interfaces |
| `<<util>>` | Light Gray | Utility/helper components |
| `<<agent>>` | Soft Blue | AI agents, autonomous components |
| `<<infra>>` | Light <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> | Infrastructure components |
| `<<external>>` | Neutral Gray | External systems |

### Arrow Macros

Use defined macros for consistent arrow styling:

```plantuml
SYNC_LINE     ' Red solid line - synchronous calls
ASYNC_LINE    ' Green dashed - async/event-based
DATA_LINE     ' <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> solid - data flow
CONTROL_LINE  ' Purple solid - control flow
OPTIONAL_LINE ' Gray dotted - optional paths
```

---

## PNG Generation

### Generating PNGs from PlantUML

Use the PlantUML JAR or online service:

```bash
# Local generation (preferred)
java -jar plantuml.jar -tpng docs/puml/diagram-name.puml

# Or use the docs script if available
./scripts/generate-diagrams.sh
```

### PNG Naming

PNG files should match their source PUML file:
- `health-verification-flow.puml` â†’ `health-verification-flow.png`

### Output Location

PNGs should be generated to:
- `docs/images/` - For markdown documentation references
- `docs/presentation/png/` - For presentation diagrams

---

## Mermaid Diagrams

### Inline in Markdown

Use fenced code blocks with `mermaid` language:

```markdown
```mermaid
graph TD
    A[Start] --> B{Decision}
    B -->|Yes| C[Action]
    B -->|No| D[End]
```
```

### Style Guidelines

1. Use clear, descriptive node labels
2. Keep diagrams focused - split large diagrams into multiple
3. Use subgraphs for logical grouping
4. Prefer `graph TD` (top-down) over `graph LR` (left-right) for readability

---

## Markdown Documentation

### File Naming

- Use kebab-case: `api-quota-checker.md`
- Use `README.md` for directory index files
- Never use spaces or special characters

### Structure

1. Start with H1 title matching the topic
2. Include brief overview paragraph
3. Use H2 for major sections
4. Use H3 for subsections
5. Include code examples where applicable

### Links

- Use relative paths for internal links: `[Status Line](./status-line.md)`
- Use absolute URLs for external links
- Verify links work before committing

Get at console.anthropic.com â†’ Settings â†’ Admin API Keys\n- **OpenAI**: `OPENAI_ADMIN_API_KEY` - Get at platform.openai.com/settings/organization/admin-keys\n- **Groq**: No public billing API yet - update `monthlySpend` manually from console.groq.com",
  "new_string": "## API Quota Monitoring\n\nAll four LLM providers update automatically via API-based or self-tracking mechanisms. No manual spend updates needed after initial key setup.\n\n### Format\n\n`[Provider$X ...]` â€” dollar amounts show live spend or remaining balance.\n\n### Provider Data Sources\n\n| Abbrev | Provider | Data Source | Setup |\n|--------|----------|-------------|-------|\n| `Gq` | Groq | BudgetTracker self-tracking | Automatic (no key needed) |\n| `Ggl` | <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> Gemini | Free tier (no tracking) | `GEMINI_API_KEY` |\n| `A` | Anthropic | Admin API (cost report) | `ANTHROPIC_ADMIN_API_KEY` |\n| `O` | OpenAI | Admin API (costs) | `OPENAI_ADMIN_API_KEY` |\n| `X` | X.AI Grok | Management API (balance) | `XAI_MANAGEMENT_KEY` + `XAI_TEAM_ID` |\n\n### Display Logic\n\n| Scenario | Display | Meaning |\n|----------|---------|---------|\n| Admin API: spend data | `A$2` | $2 spent this month (live) |\n| Admin API: with prepaid credits | `A$18` | $18 remaining of prepaid |\n| Monthly self-tracked (Groq) | `Gq$0FEB` | $0 spent in February |\n| Management API (xAI) | `X$25` | $25 remaining balance |\n| Free tier (<COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED>) | `Gglâ—` | Available (rate-limited) |\n| No admin key configured | `Oâ—‹` | Cannot get usage data |\n\n### Pie Chart Symbols\n\nUsed when percentage-based display applies (prepaid credits configured):\n\n| Symbol | Name | Remaining |\n|--------|------|-----------|\n| `â—` | Full | >87.5% |\n| `â—•` | Three-quarters | 62.5-87.5% |\n| `â—` | Half | 37.5-62.5% |\n| `â—”` | <USER_ID_REDACTED> | 12.5-37.5% |\n| `â—‹` | Empty | <12.5% or no data |\n\n### Setup\n\nRun the interactive setup script to configure API keys (one-time):\n\n```bash\nnode scripts/setup-api-keys.js\n```\n\nEach key is validated with a test API call before saving to `.env`. Groq requires no setup.\n\n### API Keys Reference\n\n| Variable | Provider | Where to Get It |\n|----------|----------|----------------|\n| `ANTHROPIC_ADMIN_API_KEY` | Anthropic | console.anthropic.com â†’ Settings â†’ Admin API Keys |\n| `OPENAI_ADMIN_API_KEY` | OpenAI | platform.openai.com/settings/organization/admin-keys |\n| `XAI_MANAGEMENT_KEY` | xAI | console.x.ai â†’ Settings â†’ Management Keys |\n| `XAI_TEAM_ID` | xAI | console.x.ai team settings URL |\n\n### How Groq Self-Tracking Works\n\nGroq has no billing API. The Docker-based `BudgetTracker` (`src/inference/BudgetTracker.js`) tracks costs from every LLM call and periodically writes to `.data/llm-usage-costs.json` (debounced, atomic write). The `api-quota-checker.js` reads this file for Groq spend. The legacy Playwright billing scraper is automatically bypassed when self-tracking data exists.\n\n### Configuration\n\nProvider credits in `config/live-logging-config.json` serve as fallbacks:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"provider_credits\": {\n    \"groq\": {\n      \"billingType\": \"monthly\",\n      \"monthlySpend\": 0,\n      \"billingMonth\": \"FEB\",\n      \"spendLimit\": null\n    },\n    \"anthropic\": { \"prepaidCredits\": 0 },\n    \"openai\": { \"prepaidCredits\": null },\n    \"xai\": { \"prepaidCredits\": 25 }\n  }\n}\n```"

### Edit - 2026-02-22 14:11:55 UTC [15:11:55 CEST]

**User Request:** # Documentation Style Guide

Enforce consistent styling for documentation artifacts (PlantUML, Mermaid, markdown, PNG diagrams).

## Instructions

When creating or modifying documentation artifacts, follow these guidelines strictly.

---

## PlantUML Diagrams (.puml)

### File Naming Convention

**CRITICAL**: Use kebab-case, descriptive names. NEVER use incremental suffixes.

**Correct**:
- `health-verification-flow.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components.puml`

**WRONG** (constraint violation):
- `health-verification-flow-2.puml`
- `knowledge-architecture-v2.puml`
- `constraint-monitor-components-new.puml`

If updating an existing diagram, **modify the existing file** rather than creating a new version.

### Standard Style Include

All PlantUML files MUST include the standard style at the top:

```plantuml
@startuml diagram-name
!include _standard-style.puml

' ... diagram content ...

@enduml
```

The style file is located at:
- `docs/puml/_standard-style.puml`
- `docs/presentation/puml/_standard-style.puml`

### Layout Guidelines

1. **Prefer vertical layouts** - Avoid excessive width that requires horizontal scrolling
2. **Use `top to bottom direction`** for most diagrams
3. **Use `left to right direction`** only for sequence diagrams or when horizontal flow is semantically meaningful
4. **Group related components** using packages or rectangles

### Component Stereotypes

Use these stereotypes for consistent coloring:

| Stereotype | Color | Use For |
|------------|-------|---------|
| `<<api>>` | Light Blue | API endpoints, REST interfaces |
| `<<core>>` | Light Green | Core business logic |
| `<<storage>>` | Light Yellow | Databases, file storage |
| `<<cli>>` | Light Pink | Command-line interfaces |
| `<<util>>` | Light Gray | Utility/helper components |
| `<<agent>>` | Soft Blue | AI agents, autonomous components |
| `<<infra>>` | Light <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> | Infrastructure components |
| `<<external>>` | Neutral Gray | External systems |

### Arrow Macros

Use defined macros for consistent arrow styling:

```plantuml
SYNC_LINE     ' Red solid line - synchronous calls
ASYNC_LINE    ' Green dashed - async/event-based
DATA_LINE     ' <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> solid - data flow
CONTROL_LINE  ' Purple solid - control flow
OPTIONAL_LINE ' Gray dotted - optional paths
```

---

## PNG Generation

### Generating PNGs from PlantUML

Use the PlantUML JAR or online service:

```bash
# Local generation (preferred)
java -jar plantuml.jar -tpng docs/puml/diagram-name.puml

# Or use the docs script if available
./scripts/generate-diagrams.sh
```

### PNG Naming

PNG files should match their source PUML file:
- `health-verification-flow.puml` â†’ `health-verification-flow.png`

### Output Location

PNGs should be generated to:
- `docs/images/` - For markdown documentation references
- `docs/presentation/png/` - For presentation diagrams

---

## Mermaid Diagrams

### Inline in Markdown

Use fenced code blocks with `mermaid` language:

```markdown
```mermaid
graph TD
    A[Start] --> B{Decision}
    B -->|Yes| C[Action]
    B -->|No| D[End]
```
```

### Style Guidelines

1. Use clear, descriptive node labels
2. Keep diagrams focused - split large diagrams into multiple
3. Use subgraphs for logical grouping
4. Prefer `graph TD` (top-down) over `graph LR` (left-right) for readability

---

## Markdown Documentation

### File Naming

- Use kebab-case: `api-quota-checker.md`
- Use `README.md` for directory index files
- Never use spaces or special characters

### Structure

1. Start with H1 title matching the topic
2. Include brief overview paragraph
3. Use H2 for major sections
4. Use H3 for subsections
5. Include code examples where applicable

### Links

- Use relative paths for internal links: `[Status Line](./status-line.md)`
- Use absolute URLs for external links
- Verify links work before committing

---

## Validation Workflow

Before committing documentation changes:

1. **PlantUML**: Verify syntax by generating PNG
2. **Mermaid**: Preview in VS Code or GitHub
3. **Markdown**: Check rendering in preview
4. **Links**: Verify all internal links work
5. **Images**: Ensure referenced images exist

---

## Common Violations to Avoid

1. **Incremental naming** (`-2`, `-v2`, `-new` suffixes)
2. **Missing style include** in PlantUML
3. **Horizontal-heavy layouts** causing scroll
4. **Orphaned images** (PNG without source PUML)
5. **Broken internal links**
6. **Inconsistent component colors** (not using stereotypes)

---

## Quick Reference

| Artifact | Location | Naming | Style |
|----------|----------|--------|-------|
| PlantUML | `docs/puml/` | kebab-case.puml | Include `_standard-style.puml` |
| PNG | `docs/images/` | match-source.png | Generated from PUML |
| Markdown | `docs/*/` | kebab-case.md | H1 title, H2 sections |
| Mermaid | Inline | N/A | graph TD preferred |

**Tool:** Edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/docs-content/guides/status-line.md",
  "old_string": "| `lib/api-quota-checker.js` | API quota provider |",
  "new_string": "| `lib/api-quota-checker.js` | API quota provider (calls Admin/Management APIs) |\n| `src/inference/BudgetTracker.js` | LLM cost tracking with file persistence (Docker) |\n| `scripts/setup-api-keys.js` | Interactive admin/management API key setup |\n| `.data/llm-usage-costs.json` | BudgetTracker cost output (Groq self-tracking) |"
}
```

**Result:** âœ… Success
**Output:** ```
The file /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/docs-content/guides/status-line.md has been updated successfully.
```

| `<<agent>>` | Soft Blue | AI agents, autonomous components |
| `<<infra>>` | Light <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> | Infrastructure components |
| `<<external>>` | Neutral Gray | External systems |

### Arrow Macros

Use defined macros for consistent arrow styling:

```plantuml
SYNC_LINE     ' Red solid line - synchronous calls
ASYNC_LINE    ' Green dashed - async/event-based
DATA_LINE     ' <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> solid - data flow
CONTROL_LINE  ' Purple solid - control flow
OPTIONAL_LINE ' Gray dotted - optional paths
```

---

## PNG Generation

### Generating PNGs from PlantUML

Use the PlantUML JAR or online service:

```bash
# Local generation (preferred)
java -jar plantuml.jar -tpng docs/puml/diagram-name.puml

# Or use the docs script if available
./scripts/generate-diagrams.sh
```

### PNG Naming

PNG files should match their source PUML file:
- `health-verification-flow.puml` â†’ `health-verification-flow.png`

### Output Location

PNGs should be generated to:
- `docs/images/` - For markdown documentation references
- `docs/presentation/png/` - For presentation diagrams

---

## Mermaid Diagrams

### Inline in Markdown

Use fenced code blocks with `mermaid` language:

```markdown
```mermaid
graph TD
    A[Start] --> B{Decision}
    B -->|Yes| C[Action]
    B -->|No| D[End]
```
```

### Style Guidelines

1. Use clear, descriptive node labels
2. Keep diagrams focused - split large diagrams into multiple
3. Use subgraphs for logical grouping
4. Prefer `graph TD` (top-down) over `graph LR` (left-right) for readability

---

## Markdown Documentation

### File Naming

- Use kebab-case: `api-quota-checker.md`
- Use `README.md` for directory index files
- Never use spaces or special characters

### Structure

1. Start with H1 title matching the topic
2. Include brief overview paragraph
3. Use H2 for major sections
4. Use H3 for subsections
5. Include code examples where applicable

### Links

- Use relative paths for internal links: `[Status Line](./status-line.md)`
- Use absolute URLs for external links
- Verify links work before committing

---

## Validation Workflow

Before committing documentation changes:

1. **PlantUML**: Verify syntax by generating PNG
2. **Mermaid**: Preview in VS Code or GitHub
3. **Markdown**: Check rendering in preview
4. **Links**: Verify all internal links work
5. **Images**: Ensure referenced images exist

---

## Common Violations to Avoid

1. **Incremental naming** (`-2`, `-v2`, `-new` suffixes)
2. **Missing style include** in PlantUML
3. **Horizontal-heavy layouts** causing scroll
4. **Orphaned images** (PNG without source PUML)
5. **Broken internal links**
6. **Inconsistent component colors** (not using stereotypes)

---

## Quick Reference

| Artifact | Location | Naming | Style |
|----------|----------|--------|-------|
| PlantUML | `docs/puml/` | kebab-case.puml | Include `_standard-style.puml` |
| PNG | `docs/images/` | match-source.png | Generated from PUML |
| Markdown | `docs/*/` | kebab-case.md | H1 title, H2 sections |
| Mermaid | Inline | N/A | graph TD preferred |

**Tool:** Edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>h-system/README.md",
  "old_string": "- `[Gq$0FEB A$0 O$0 X$25]` - API quota status (Groq $2 spent in Jan, etc.)",
  "new_string": "- `[Gq$0FEB A$0 O$0 X$25]` - API quota (live spend/balance from APIs)"
}
```

**Result:** âœ… Success
**Output:** ```
The file <AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>h-system/README.md has been updated successfully.
```
